| 1:19:45| I found a more recent case than the BFI case| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4785)|
| 1:19:48| called Rogers Group versus County of Franklin.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4788)|
| 1:19:52| And in that case, the County of Franklin had adopted a zoning ordinance,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4792)|
| 1:19:56| and it gave their Board of Zoning Appeals the right to hear appeals,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4796)|
| 1:20:01| and I will read the language to you.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4801)|
| 1:20:07| To hear and decide appeals where it is alleged by the appellant| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4807)|
| 1:20:10| there is an error in any order, requirement, permit, decisions,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4810)|
| 1:20:13| implication, determination, or refusal made by the building commissioner| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4813)|
| 1:20:17| or other administrative official in carrying out the enforcement| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4817)|
| 1:20:20| of any provision of this resolution.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4820)|
| 1:20:22| Now, that's the same language that is used in the state law| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4822)|
| 1:20:25| in referring to the authority of the Board of Zoning Appeals,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4825)|
| 1:20:29| that very language.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4829)|
| 1:20:31| And so I want to stress, again, it says,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4831)|
| 1:20:33| to hear the appeals of decisions made by the building commissioner| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4833)|
| 1:20:37| or other administrative official.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4837)|
| 1:20:40| That's the language.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4840)|
| 1:20:41| In this case, in Rogers Group case, the question was directly asked,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4841)|
| 1:20:46| when the language says other administrative official,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4846)|
| 1:20:50| does that include the planning commission?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4850)|
| 1:20:53| And the Court of Appeals said no.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4853)|
| 1:20:55| And they said no for reasons that have everything to do| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4855)|
| 1:20:58| with all the rules of statutory construction.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4858)|
| 1:21:00| When you are construing a statute, you do not stretch the meaning of words.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4860)|
| 1:21:05| You give them their ordinary, natural meaning.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4865)|
| 1:21:08| You don't assume that a statute overlooked something.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4868)|
| 1:21:11| You assume that every word was used with purpose.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4871)|
| 1:21:14| But the Court of Appeals said, and what I would say,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4874)|
| 1:21:16| is that if the intent of the legislature was to say that the Board of Zoning| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4876)|
| 1:21:23| Appeals had authority to hear appeals from the planning commission,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4883)|
| 1:21:27| it would have said the planning commission.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4887)|
| 1:21:30| The planning commission is mentioned multiple places in the same statute,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4890)|
| 1:21:34| and yet they never say the planning commission.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4894)|
| 1:21:37| They say the building commissioner or other administrative official.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4897)|
| 1:21:41| So I do not believe that that language is broad enough to implicate the BZA.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-220822-zoning?start=4901)|
